<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Learn Effective Service Leadership with Enneagram</h2> </div>

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-702aa62 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="702aa62" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">This two-day course equips professionals with practical leadership skills enhanced by the Enneagram framework. With 16 hours of learning, this program focuses on improving self-awareness, adapting leadership styles, and building high-performance teams by understanding personality types to improve collaboration and engagement.</span></p> </div>

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e89dd82 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="e89dd82" data-element_type="container">

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">What is Enneagram?</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4fcfb62 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="4fcfb62" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;"><img decoding="async" class="wp-image-23762 alignleft" src="http://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-300x298.png" alt="" width="340" height="338" srcset="https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-300x298.png 300w, https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-1024x1017.png 1024w, https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-150x150.png 150w, https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-768x763.png 768w, https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2-1536x1526.png 1536w, https://theqdacademy.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/enneagram-example-diagram2.png 1556w" sizes="(max-width: 340px) 100vw, 340px" />The Enneagram is a personality framework that maps out nine distinct types of people — each with its own core motivations, fears, and ways of thinking, feeling, and behaving.</span></p><p><strong><span style="color: #094744;"><span style="font-style: inherit;">How Does Enneagram Help Leaders?</span></span></strong></p><p><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">With Enneagram, leaders can understand the hidden patterns behind how their team members communicate, make decisions, and respond to stress.</span></p><p><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">For example, a manager might learn that one team member (a Type 6 Loyalist) thrives with structure and reassurance, while another (a Type 8 Challenger) values autonomy and directness.</span></p><p><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">That same manager, being a Type 2 Helper, may naturally overextend themselves or avoid setting firm boundaries in an effort to stay supportive. </span><span style="font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">By understanding both their own tendencies and those of their team, the leader can communicate more effectively, set clearer expectations, and create a more balanced, high-performing environment.</span></p> </div>
</div>
</div>

<script type='text/javascript'>
const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
if( lazyloadBackground ) {
lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
}
lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
}
});
}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
} );
};
const events = [
'DOMContentLoaded',
'elementor/lazyload/observe',
];
events.forEach( ( event ) => {
document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
} );
</script>
